## ğŸ¤” What is Nano Banana Pro?

**Nano Banana Pro** is Google's latest multimodal AI model featuring:

- ğŸ¯ **Multimodal Understanding** - Process text, images, and video
- ğŸ¨ **High-Quality Generation** - Photorealistic to artistic styles
- âš¡ **Fast Iteration** - Quick edits and variations
- ğŸŒˆ **Diverse Styles** - From pixel art to oil paintings
- ğŸ”§ **Precise Control** - Detailed composition and lighting
- ğŸ“ **Complex Scenes** - Multi-object, multi-character rendering

ğŸ“š **Learn More:** [Nano Banana Pro: 10 Real Cases](https://youmind.com/blog/nano-banana-pro-10-real-cases)

### ğŸš€ Raycast Integration

Some prompts support **dynamic arguments** using [Raycast Snippets](https://raycast.com/help/snippets) syntax. Look for the ğŸš€ Raycast Friendly badge!

**Example:**
```
A quote card with "{argument name="quote" default="Stay hungry, stay foolish"}"
by {argument name="author" default="Steve Jobs"}
```

When used in Raycast, you can dynamically replace the arguments for quick iterations!

### No. 1: High-Definition Vintage Flash Portrait Prompt

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A detailed JSON prompt designed for Nano Banana Pro to transform an input photo into a high-definition, warm-toned vintage portrait. It specifies strict identity lock rules, realistic skin texture preservation, vintage color grading, and a specific indoor hallway scene with flash lighting and composition details.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
{
"meta":{
"quality":"High-Definition",
"type":"Evening indoor flash portrait",
"ratio":"4:5 vertical",
"device":"iPhone 16 Pro",
"style_reference":"Transform the INPUT PHOTO into this exact aesthetic.",
"look":"Evening flash, warm-toned vintage, real grain, realistic skin texture (NO smoothing)."
},

"identity_lock":{
"preserve_face": true,
"strict": true,
"rules":[
"The face MUST remain IDENTICAL to the input photo.",
"No changes to facial structure, proportions, expression, or identity.",
"No smoothing, no beautify, no retouch, no AI facial alterations."
]
},

"skin_texture_rules":{
"keep_texture": true,
"no_smoothing": true,
"no_blur": true,
"realistic_details": "natural texture preserved.",
"flash_behavior":"Flash highlights should reveal texture, not hide it."
},

"vintage_effect":{
"warmth":"+18",
"contrast":"+22",
"highlights":"-5",
"shadows":"+12",
"grain":"Medium (film-like)",
"vignette":"Soft",
"color_grade":"Warm beige vintage tint",
"sharpness":"Slightly reduced to mimic old camera softness"
},

"global_context":{
"scene_description":"Indoor hallway with wall decor, mirror reflection, white walls and warm flash lighting.",
"time_of_day":"Evening",
"lighting":"Direct warm flash illuminating the subject with strong falloff into the background.",
"environment_details":[
"Mirror behind the subject with reflection visible.",
"White paneled walls.",
"Marble/stone console table with a floral arrangement.",
"Soft shadows created by harsh flash."
]
},

"composition":{
"camera_angle":"Eye-level, straight-on portrait",
"framing":"Knees-up full portrait",
"pose":"Body leaning slightly forward with one hand on console table and the other arm across the torso.",
"expression":"Confident, pouty, soft glamorous gaze.",
"flash_effect":"Glossy highlights on skin and dress."
},

"subject":{
"makeup":{
"style":"Soft glam.",
"lips":"Pink-brown gloss with warm undertone.",
"eyes":"Eyeliner + lashes.",
"blush":"Warm peach."
},
"skin":"Natural undertone, realistic texture, NOT smoothed.",
"outfit":{
"dress":"White mini halter dress with deep neckline and satin-like shine.",
"fabric_behavior":"Flash creates bright reflections and visible folds."
}
},

"background_objects":[
{
"id":"mirror",
"description":"Large wall mirror reflecting the subject's pose.",
"lighting":"Flash reflection visible but subdued."
},
{
"id":"flowers",
"description":"Vibrant bouquet on the table (yellow, purple, green)."
},
{
"id":"wall",
"description":"White paneled wall with framed signage."
}
],

"rules":{
"identity_constant": true,
"no_face_change": true,
"no_ai_artifacts": true,
"realism":"Ultra realistic evening flash aesthetic with vintage tones."
}
}
Use the uploaded photo as the input image. Generate the image.
```

### No. 2: Fairy-Core Mirror Selfie in a Floral Cafe

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A highly specific image generation prompt for Gemini Nano Banana Pro, requiring strict adherence to a reference photo's facial identity. The prompt details a full-body mirror selfie pose (squatting low) in a romantic, fairy-core aesthetic, specifying the pastel pink corset dress, butterfly-adorned heels, and the charming floral cafe interior setting, aiming for 8K photorealism.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
{
  "image_generation_prompt": {
    "subject": {
      "reference_adherence": "Strictly match the provided reference photo face exactly",
      "facial_features": [
        "Preserve exact face shape",
        "Match eye structure and eyebrow shape",
        "Retain lip shape and natural color"
      ],
      "hair": "{argument name="hair color" default="black"}, exact hairstyle from reference",
      "makeup": "Natural style as per reference",
      "expression": "Soft, calm, looking at phone screen"
    },

    "apparel": {
      "main_garment": "Soft pastel {argument name="dress color" default="pink"}, romantic corset-style mini dress inspired by a fairy-core aesthetic. Off-shoulder neckline with delicate gathered fabric, lace-up corset bodice that cinches the waist, and a flowy chiffon skirt with layered movement. Long, sheer, flared sleeves that drape gracefully with light fabric transparency. Dress matches exactly the reference pink dress in color, silhouette, and romantic style.",
      "fabric_physics": "Lightweight chiffon and satin blend, airy movement, natural folds, soft wind-like flow",
      "footwear": "Pastel blush {argument name="shoe color" default="pink"} satin high-heeled sandals with a square toe. Delicate thin straps adorned with embroidered 3D butterfly appliquÃ©s across the front and ankle straps. Slim feminine heel, elegant fairy-core aesthetic, matching exactly the reference butterfly heels in color, texture, and romantic detail.",
      "accessories": [
        "Silver necklace",
        "Silver bracelet",
        "Silver rings"
      ]
    },

    "pose_and_action": {
      "type": "Full-body mirror selfie",
      "stance": "Squatting low gracefully, one knee forward, leaning slightly toward mirror",
      "head_position": "Tilted slightly downward",
      "hands": {
        "right_hand": "Holding phone vertically in front of face",
        "left_hand": "Resting gently on knee"
      },
      "props": "Smartphone with soft pink phone case, soft pastel tone, minimal design"
    },

    "environment": {
      "location": "Charming floral cafe interior",
      "background": "Romantic European-style floral cafe with stone-textured walls, hanging wicker baskets, dried flower arrangements, pastel floral bouquets, vintage wooden shelves, rustic beams, and soft decorative mirrors. Warm neutral stone tones mixed with soft pinks, greens, creams, and lavender florals. Cozy, aesthetic, feminine atmosphere.",
      "flooring": "Vintage patterned tile floor with subtle reflections"
    },

    "lighting_and_atmosphere": {
      "quality": "Soft, ambient cafe lighting with gentle highlights",
      "mood": "Feminine, romantic, elegant, fairy-core, social media aesthetic"
    },

    "technical_specifications": {
      "quality": "8K resolution, photorealistic, high fidelity",
      "focus": "Sharp focus on face and outfit",
      "perspective": "Eye-level mirror perspective",
      "aspect_ratio": "4:5"
    }
  }
}
```

### No. 3: Intimate Photorealistic FaceTime Portrait Prompt

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A highly specific JSON prompt for Nano Banana Pro to generate an ultra-high-resolution, photorealistic image mimicking an intimate FaceTime video call capture. It details the scene (bedroom, resting on a pillow), composition (extreme close-up on eyes/forehead), subject appearance (natural texture, bed hair), and includes an iOS FaceTime thumbnail overlay with a red heart emoji.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
{ "task": "intimate_photorealistic_facetime_portrait", "output": { "type": "single_image", "resolution": "ultra_high_resolution", "realism": "natural_iphone_photography", "quality": "front_camera_selfie", "retouching": "none_skin_texture_preserved" }, "scene": { "location": "bedroom", "setting": "quiet_private_moment", "environment": { "surface": "white_pillow", "background": "soft_blurred_neutral", "lighting": "ambient_natural_light" } }, "composition": { "shot_type": "extreme_close_up", "camera_angle": "top_down_resting_angle", "framing": "eyes_and_forehead_dominant", "crop": "vertical", "moment": "sleepy_facetime_capture" }, "subject": { "role": "primary_subject", "gender": "male", "age_range": "young_adult", "pose": { "head": "resting_on_pillow", "eyes": "half_open_relaxed" }, "appearance": { "skin": "natural_texture_visible", "hair": "slightly_messy_bed_hair", "facial_hair": "optional_light_stubble", "makeup": "none" }, "expression": "soft_intimate" }, "interaction": { "context": "facetime_video_call", "overlay": { "picture_in_picture": { "position": "top_right", "subject": { "role": "girlfriend", "gender": "female", "age_range": "young_adult", "expression": "gentle_smile", "appearance": { "skin": "natural", "makeup": "minimal", "hair": "natural_loose" } }, "style": "ios_facetime_thumbnail" }, "emoji": { "type": "red_heart", "placement": "center_forehead_of_main_subject", "style": "iphone_emoji_overlay" } } }, "camera": { "device": "iPhone", "lens": "front_camera", "focal_length_equivalent": "26mm", "focus": "eyes_and_skin", "depth_of_field": "very_shallow_natural" }, "lighting": { "type": "soft_diffused", "source": "ambient_room_light", "contrast": "low", "shadows": "gentle" }, "color_grading": { "tone": "warm_neutral", "contrast": "soft", "saturation": "natural" }, "negative_prompt": [ "beauty_filters", "over_smoothing", "plastic_skin", "studio_lighting", "harsh_contrast", "distorted_face", "ai_artifacts", "cartoon_style" ] }
```

### No. 4: Gallery Wall Portrait with Identity Lock

![Language-ZH](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-ZH-blue)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A prompt designed for image generation that uses a reference photo to maintain the subject's identity while placing them in a dramatic, high-fashion setting. The subject is framed against a seamless wall covered entirely in black and white portraits of themselves, emphasizing a cinematic, ultra-photorealistic quality.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
Based on [Reference Photo Person]
A high-quality 9:16 vertical portrait, 4k resolution. 
**Framing:** Medium-long shot (framed from the knees up, focusing on torso and head). 
**Subject:** The woman from the reference image, standing in 3/4 profile facing left, looking at the lens. She wears a structured black long trench coat. 
**Background:** An infinite, edge-to-edge gallery wall completely covered in a dense, seamless grid of black and white fashion portraits of herself. The photo wall fills 100% of the background frame behind her. No floor visible, no ceiling visible, just the texture of the photos. 
**Lighting:** Even, professional gallery lighting highlighting the coat's texture and the details of the background prints. 
**Quality:** Ultra-photorealistic, sharp focus, cinematic depth.
--ar 9:16 --v 6.0
```

#### ğŸ–¼ï¸ Generated Images

##### Image 1

<div align="center">
<img src="https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766238100501_aik8te_G8kBFCuXEAA5m5o.jpg" width="600" alt="Gallery Wall Portrait with Identity Lock - Image 1">
</div>

##### Image 2

<div align="center">
<img src="https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766238100825_9udbml_G8kBFCuW8AAcSTu.jpg" width="600" alt="Gallery Wall Portrait with Identity Lock - Image 2">

### No. 8: High-End Conceptual Product Magazine Photography Prompt

![Language-ZH](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-ZH-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A detailed, multi-section prompt for Nano Banana Pro designed to generate high-end, glossy magazine editorial photography of a unique, unexpected functional object conceptualized and designed by a specified brand. It includes strict requirements for concept invention, ultra-premium materials, cinematic studio lighting, and precise layout elements like logo and descriptive text placement.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
{argument name="Brand Name" default="[Brand Name]"}: 
A high-end, glossy conceptual art magazine editorial photograph showcasing a unique, unexpected functional object conceptualized and designed by the brand.

**1. Concept and Object (AI Invention):** 
Based on the specified brand's design philosophy, heritage, and material vocabulary, the AI must invent a new type of practical product (not standard clothing, shoes, or bags). Examples may include home goods, tech accessories, tools, or sports equipment, reinterpreted through the brand's perspective. The object should feel sculptural yet functional.

**2. Materials and Details (Ultra High-End):** 
The object is made of high-end, highly tactile materials characteristic of the brand (e.g., oxidized exotic leather, brushed aerospace-grade titanium, sculptural matte ceramic, molded carbon fiber, or technical haute couture textiles). Every detail must be extremely realistic: visible stitching, microscopic material textures, precision engraving, and complex texture contrasts.

**3. Photography and Lighting (Cinematic Studio):** 
Shot with a medium format Phase One camera paired with a 100mm macro lens. Extremely shallow depth of field, with the main object sharply focused and the background blurred to a creamy smoothness. Lighting is exquisite studio softbox illumination: soft, enveloping fill light combined with precise contour light to highlight outlines and material textures.

**4. Environment:** 
Seamless, flawless, pure, ultra-light-toned studio cyclorama background (e.g., desaturated mint green, light pink, or yellowish-white), with no shadows.

**5. Layout and UI Elements (Strict Placement):** 
- **Bottom Right:** The brand's small, low-key, monochromatic gray logo. 
- **Bottom Left:** Small, extremely simple monochromatic gray text describing the invented product. Font style similar to Manrope Regular, with extremely tight tracking (kerning) and balanced line spacing. Example format: "CONCEPT STUDY: [AI inserts invented product name]. MATERIAL: [AI inserts primary material]. SS25."
```

### No. 15: Vintage Evening Flash Portrait Transformation Prompt

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

An extensive JSON prompt for Gemini Nano Banana, designed for image-to-image transformation. It applies a warm-toned, film-like vintage aesthetic with harsh flash lighting and realistic grain to an input photo, while strictly preserving the subject's facial identity and skin texture (no smoothing or AI alterations).

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
{
"meta":{
"quality":"High-Definition",
"type":"Evening indoor flash portrait",
"ratio":"4:5 vertical",
"device":"iPhone 16 Pro",
"style_reference":"Transform the INPUT PHOTO into this exact aesthetic.",
"look":"Evening flash, warm-toned vintage, real grain, realistic skin texture (NO smoothing)."
},

"identity_lock":{
"preserve_face": true,
"strict": true,
"rules":[
"The face MUST remain IDENTICAL to the input photo.",
"No changes to facial structure, proportions, expression, or identity.",
"No smoothing, no beautify, no retouch, no AI facial alterations."
]
},

"skin_texture_rules":{
"keep_texture": true,
"no_smoothing": true,
"no_blur": true,
"realistic_details": "natural texture preserved.",
"flash_behavior":"Flash highlights should reveal texture, not hide it."
},

"vintage_effect":{
"warmth":"{argument name="warmth" default="+18"}",
"contrast":"{argument name="contrast" default="+22"}",
"highlights":"{argument name="highlights" default="-5"}",
"shadows":"{argument name="shadows" default="+12"}",
"grain":"{argument name="grain" default="Medium (film-like)"}",
"vignette":"{argument name="vignette" default="Soft"}",
"color_grade":"{argument name="color grade" default="Warm beige vintage tint"}",
"sharpness":"{argument name="sharpness" default="Slightly reduced to mimic old camera softness"}"
},

"global_context":{
"scene_description":"{argument name="scene description" default="Indoor hallway with wall decor, mirror reflection, white walls and warm flash lighting."}",
"time_of_day":"{argument name="time of day" default="Evening"}",
"lighting":"{argument name="lighting" default="Direct warm flash illuminating the subject with strong falloff into the background."}",
"environment_details":[
"{argument name="environment detail 1" default="Mirror behind the subject with reflection visible."}",
"{argument name="environment detail 2" default="White paneled walls."}",
"{argument name="environment detail 3" default="Marble/stone console table with a floral arrangement."}",
"{argument name="environment detail 4" default="Soft shadows created by harsh flash."}"
]
},

"composition":{
"camera_angle":"{argument name="camera angle" default="Eye-level, straight-on portrait"}",
"framing":"{argument name="framing" default="Knees-up full portrait"}",
"pose":"{argument name="pose" default="Body leaning slightly forward with one hand on console table and the other arm across the torso."}",
"expression":"{argument name="expression" default="Confident, pouty, soft glamorous gaze."}",
"flash_effect":"{argument name="flash effect" default="Glossy highlights on skin and dress."}"
},

"subject":{
"makeup":{
"style":"{argument name="makeup style" default="Soft glam."}",
"lips":"{argument name="lips" default="Pink-brown gloss with warm undertone."}",
"eyes":"{argument name="eyes" default="Eyeliner + lashes."}",
"blush":"{argument name="blush" default="Warm peach."}"
},
"skin":"{argument name="skin" default="Natural undertone, realistic texture, NOT smoothed."}",
"outfit":{
"dress":"{argument name="dress" default="White mini halter dress with deep neckline and satin-like shine."}",
"fabric_behavior":"{argument name="fabric behavior" default="Flash creates bright reflections and visible folds."}"
}
},

"background_objects":[
{
"id":"mirror",
"description":"{argument name="mirror description" default="Large wall mirror reflecting the subject's pose."}",
"lighting":"{argument name="mirror lighting" default="Flash reflection visible but subdued."}"
},
{
"id":"flowers",
"description":"{argument name="flowers description" default="Vibrant bouquet on the table (yellow, purple, green)."}"
},
{
"id":"wall",
"description":"{argument name="wall description" default="White paneled wall with framed signage."}"
}
],

"rules":{
"identity_constant": true,
"no_face_change": true,
"no_ai_artifacts": true,
"realism":"{argument name="realism" default="Ultra realistic evening flash aesthetic with vintage tones."}"
}
}
Use the uploaded photo as the input image. Generate the image.
```

#### ğŸ–¼ï¸ Generated Images

### No. 26: Culinary Periodic Table Display Board Generator

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A complex instructional prompt designed to generate a visual representation of a dish's flavor profile in the style of a scientific periodic table. It requires analyzing a dish's ingredients and flavor compounds, then rendering a detailed display board with color-coded compartments, molecular structures, and a handwritten recipe, combining chemistry aesthetics with product design.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
<instruction> 
Input A is a famous dish (photo or dish name). Analyze the dish's complete ingredient breakdown, primary flavor compounds, chemical interactions, and scientific basis for why ingredients work together.
Optional Input B is a style reference (laboratory equipment / tech product packaging). If missing, choose scientific periodic table meets Apple product design aesthetic.
Goal: Grid-format display board (20"x16") in periodic table structure, with each ingredient in its own compartment labeled with both culinary and scientific information, color-coded by flavor profile.
Rules:

Brushed aluminum, white acrylic, or frosted glass backing
20-30 small clear compartments in periodic table grid layout
Each compartment contains: ingredient specimen, common name, scientific name, primary flavor molecule
Color-coded borders: umami (red), sweet (pink), sour (yellow), bitter (green), fat (orange), aromatic (purple)
Center "legend" section: 3D molecular structure diagram of signature compound
Lower corner: actual handwritten recipe on aged vellum or parchment under glass
AR markers for scanning to see animated 3D molecule models
Clean sans-serif typography (like Helvetica or Futura)
Minimal design with generous white space
Include atomic-style "numbers" for each ingredient showing ratio/importance

Output: ONE image, 4:5 clean product photography style with soft shadows on pure white background
</instruction>
```

### No. 37: E-Girl Mirror Selfie with Deep Depth of Field

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A highly technical JSON prompt for generating an 'E-Girl Mirror Selfie' with a minimalist goth style. It specifies engine configuration, including LoRA slots and sampling settings, but its core instruction is to enforce a deep depth of field (f/11) so that the subject, bed texture, and background wall are all sharp, contrasting the typical shallow depth of field in portraits.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
{
  "meta": {
    "project": "Egirl_FrogPose_PinkHK_Flux_V4.2",
    "target_engine": "Flux.1 [dev] / Nano Banana Pro",
    "version": "4.2.0 (Everything in Focus - f/11)",
    "created_at": "2025-12-18T20:55:00Z"
  },
  "engine_configuration": {
    "model": {
      "base": "flux1-dev.safetensors",
      "quantization": "fp8 / nf4",
      "vae": "ae.safetensors"
    },
    "lora_slots": [
      {
        "name": "Realism_LoRA_v2 (Optional)",
        "strength": 0.5,
        "note": "Enhances porcelain skin tone and fabric textures."
      }
    ],
    "sampling": {
      "sampler_name": "euler",
      "scheduler": "simple",
      "steps": 28,
      "guidance_scale": 2.5,
      "shift": 1.0
    },
    "dimensions": {
      "width": 1024,
      "height": 1536,
      "aspect_ratio": "2:3",
      "megapixel_class": "1.5MP"
    }
  },
  "prompt_construction": {
    "narrative_layer": {
      "style": "E-Girl Mirror Selfie / Minimalist Goth",
      "instruction": "Capture a sharp, full-body mirror selfie of a young woman sitting in a frog pose on a bed, focusing on the midriff and the pink phone case.",
      "subject_flow": "A pale 19-21 year old woman with black wolf-cut hair sitting on a grey bed with knees up, holding a pink Hello Kitty phone."
    },
    "texture_layer": {
      "skin_physics": "pale porcelain skin, smooth texture, rosy blush, glossy lips, e-girl eyeliner",
      "fabric_physics": "ribbed knit texture of black tube top, metal grommets on belt, cotton texture of white socks, quilted grey duvet",
      "environment_physics": "SHARP DETAILS ON BACKGROUND: glass mirror reflection, white wall texture, window glass, grey fabric folds"
    },
    "camera_physics": {
      "lens_imperfections": "smartphone camera aesthetic, high fidelity",
      "focus": "DEEP DEPTH OF FIELD (f/11) - NO BLUR. The woman, the bed texture, and the background wall are all sharp.",
      "settings": "Smartphone Simulation, 24mm Lens, 1/60s, ISO 300 (Diffused Window Light)"
    },
    "color_grading": {
      "white_balance": "Cool Natural (Diffused Window Light)",
      "shadows": "Soft shadows defining the midriff",
      "highlights": "Soft highlights on skin and glossy phone case"
    }
  },
  "final_prompt_string": "A candid raw mirror selfie photograph shot on Smartphone f/11. Deep depth of field, everything in focus. A very slim 19-21 year old woman with pale porcelain skin and black hair with bangs (wolf cut) sitting on a dark grey bed in a 'frog pose' (knees bent, high and wide apart). She leans back slightly. She wears a black ribbed strapless tube top exposing her toned midriff, a low-rise black mini skirt with a heavy silver grommet belt, and white ankle socks with red Hello Kitty embroidery. She holds a phone with a light pink 3D Hello Kitty case. Dramatic e-girl eyeliner and glossy lips. Background is sharp and detailed: messy grey duvet and a plain white wall are clearly visible with no bokeh. "
```

### No. 41: Photorealistic Portrait with Shallow Depth of Field

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A highly specific prompt for generating a photorealistic portrait of a young Asian woman in a black pinstriped shirt dress and sheer thigh-high stockings. It details the pose, environment (sheer curtains), lighting (warm, soft indoor), and precise camera settings (focal length, aperture, shutter speed, ISO) to achieve a shallow depth of field and a polished, slightly candid aesthetic.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
A photorealistic portrait of a young Asian woman with voluminous, long, wavy black hair and fair skin. She is wearing thin-rimmed, round glasses and has a playful expression, winking one eye with a subtle smile. Outfit: She is dressed in a black, long-sleeved button-down shirt dress with thin white vertical pinstripes. She is wearing sheer black thigh-high stockings. Pose: She is seated in a curved, cream-colored leather armchair. Her body is angled slightly forward. Her right hand is raised, with long manicured fingers delicately touching her cheek and jawline in a playful, posing gesture. Environment: The background features soft, floor-length beige or off-white sheer curtains, suggesting an indoor hotel room or bedroom setting at night. Lighting & Style: Warm, soft indoor lighting that creates gentle highlights on her hair and the silky texture of the shirt. High-resolution photography, sharp focus on the face, slightly candid but polished aesthetic. Camera Angle: Slightly high angle (tilted down about 10â€“15 degrees), seated eye-level. Focal Length: 35mm or 50mm. (This creates a natural perspective without too much distortion, typical of high-end smartphone portraits or standard portrait lenses). Aperture: f/2.0 to f/2.8. (This provides a shallow depth of field, keeping her face and hand in sharp focus while softly blurring the texture of the curtains in the background). Shutter Speed: 1/60s or 1/100s. (Standard for indoor handheld shots to avoid motion blur). ISO: 400 to 800. (Slightly higher sensitivity to account for the warm, dim indoor lighting without introducing too much grain). Lighting Setup: Soft key light from the front-top (likely a ceiling fixture or ring light), creating the specular highlights on the nose and forehead.
```

```
      ]
```
```
    },
```

### No. 59: Three Identity-Locked Photorealistic Portraits

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A collection of three distinct prompts, all focused on generating highly photorealistic portraits while strictly preserving the facial identity of an uploaded reference image. They cover different styles: an extreme close-up beauty shot, a cinematic travel portrait in a snowy alpine train, and a retro vintage 90s look with a red dress and flowers.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
Prompt 1:
"A hyper-realistic, extreme close-up beauty portrait of a stunning woman. She is raising her arm to cover the left side of her face, wearing a vibrant red ribbed-knit sweater. Only one mesmerizing hazel-green eye is visible, featuring dramatic black winged eyeliner, gold glitter eyeshadow, and long lashes. Her lips are full and painted with a matte red lipstick that matches the sweater perfectly. Flawless airbrushed skin, soft studio lighting, high fashion editorial style, sharp focus on the eye no facial change same as it is on the reference picture."

Prompt 2:
"Create a highly photorealistic, cinematic travel portrait of a young woman whose facial identity exactly matches the uploaded reference image, with 100% preservation of facial structure, proportions, skin texture, eye shape, lips, nose, brows, moles, and natural expression. She has a soft, relaxed smile with calm eyes and is gently looking toward the camera. Her pose shows her leaning out of a train window, with both arms resting comfortably on the window frame and her upper body slightly leaned forward in a relaxed, cozy posture.
She has dark brown straight hair worn loose and slightly tucked under a white knitted winter beanie with a soft knit texture. Her makeup is natural winter-style, featuring an even fair skin tone, light blush, soft eyeliner, natural lashes, and subtle pink lips. She is wearing a cream or off-white cozy winter sweater made of soft, warm knit fabric suitable for cold weather.
The scene is set inside a red panoramic train traveling through snowy alpine mountains. The background includes snow-covered pine trees, mountain slopes blanketed in snow, curving red train cars visible behind her, and thick snow piled along the tracks, clearly conveying a winter landscape. Lighting is natural cold daylight with soft diffusion, cool winter tones, gentle highlights on the face, and natural shadows.
The overall style is a cinematic travel portrait with a DSLR photography look, moderate depth of field that keeps the subject sharp while preserving scenic background detail, and a peaceful, cozy, adventurous winter travel mood. Use high-resolution rendering with realistic skin texture, high detail, and cool winter color grading with soft contrast, maintaining strict identity lock to the reference image throughout."

Prompt 3:
"Create A hyper-realistic person (Retro vintage, grainy but bright aesthetic. A girl(face exactly same as the reference image) wearing a perfect red wine colored red frock, holding a A bunch of 10-12 flowers of roses in her hands. The style feels like a 90s movie, romantic, wind blowing girl. She is standing against a solid wall with deep shadows and dramatic contrast, mysterious and artistic atmosphere."
```

### No. 62: Travel Itinerary Illustration Generation Prompt

![Language-JA](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-JA-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A detailed prompt for Nano Banana Pro to generate a 'hand-drawn travel itinerary' illustration based on a character reference image. It includes sections for customizable input (character features, title, destination, schedule, and packing list) and strict specifications for the image generation style, layout (vertical A4, grid background, timeline composition), content reflection (5-6 small cut illustrations per schedule item, character consistency, expression reflection), and decorative elements.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
Generate an illustration image in the style of a travel itinerary according to the following requirements.

## 1. Input Settings
** (Please rewrite this section. If left blank, it will be treated as "Leave it to AI")**
- **Character Features**: {argument name="Character Features" default="A girl with brown short hair, wearing a black cloak"}
- **Name (for Title)**: {argument name="Name for Title" default="Complete Guide to the Donut Museum!"}
- **Tourist Destination**: {argument name="Tourist Destination" default="Donut Museum"}
- **Schedule**: [
Format: "Time : Place/Action : Short Comment (Situation or Feeling at the time)"
]
- **Packing List**:

## 2. Image Generation Specifications
You are an illustrator for a travel magazine. Based on the settings above, draw one "hand-drawn travel itinerary" in the following style.

**ã€Style and Compositionã€‘**
- **Aspect Ratio**: Vertical (Vertical format close to A4 paper ratio)
- **Background**: Graph paper (grid notebook) texture.
- **Art Style**: Warm, hand-drawn style illustration like the reference image (watercolor, marker, colored pencil touch).
- **Layout**:
- Place the title prominently at the top.
- Timeline composition connected by arrows flowing from the top left to the bottom right.
- Memo illustration of the "Packing List" in the bottom right or an empty space.

**ã€Content and Comment Reflectionã€‘**
- Draw each item in the specified "Schedule" as **5-6 small cut illustrations**.
- Maintain **character consistency**.
- **Comment Reflection**:
- Reflect the content of the "Short Comment" in the schedule in the character's **expression and pose** (e.g., if "delicious," the cheeks should be relaxed; if "excited," the eyes should sparkle).
- Place a **handwritten-style text space (like a speech bubble, sign, or writing in the margin)** next to or below each panel for the comment.
- *The text in the image must be accurate Japanese. Use a font that looks like handwritten notes.*

**ã€Decorationã€‘**
- Overall cheerful and pop atmosphere.
- Decorate with masking tape, stamps, handwritten arrows, and musical note marks.
```

### No. 63: Anamorphic Graphite Sketch Illusion Prompt

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A highly complex image generation prompt for Nano-Banana Pro, designed to create a photorealistic image of a graphite sketch that appears to be reaching out of the paper (anamorphic illusion). The prompt requires a reference image for the subject's identity and details the artistic style, demanding monochromatic greyscale for the subject and realistic colors for the surrounding drawing tools and rustic wooden desk.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
{
  "subject_core": {
    "demographics": "[STRICTLY FOLLOW REFERENCE IMAGE]: Age, gender, and ethnicity must match the uploaded source photo exactly. Rendered as a hyper-realistic graphite sketch.",
    "body_type": "Matches reference image physique, appearing to lean forward out of the 2D plane",
    "facial_features": "High-fidelity graphite translation of the reference face; shading emphasizes specific bone structure and unique traits from the source photo; eyes detailed with paper-white catchlights",
    "hair": "Matches reference image hairstyle and texture exactly, rendered with varying pencil pressure (hatching and cross-hatching)"
  },
  "subject_styling": {
    "makeup_grooming": "Matches reference image grooming standards; skin texture converted to realistic pencil grain and stippling",
    "expression": "Matches reference image expression (e.g., focused, smiling, or neutral), intense gaze directed relative to the viewer",
    "pose_action": "Anamorphic illusion: The subject's hand (drawn in graphite) creates a 3D effect, appearing to reach out of the flat paper surface, holding a realistic wooden pencil"
  },
  "wardrobe": {
    "top": "Matches clothing from reference image, textures converted to graphite cross-hatching to imply fabric weight",
    "bottom": "N/A (cropped or fading into the white of the paper)",
    "footwear": "N/A",
    "accessories": "Any distinct accessories from the reference photo rendered in sketch format"
  },
  "environment_context": {
    "location": "Macro view of a textured, heavy-tooth white sketchbook page resting on a dark rustic wooden surface",
    "background_elements": "Real-world objects resting on the paper to sell the scale: a worn white block eraser, a metal pencil sharpener, scattered cedar wood pencil shavings, smudge of graphite dust",
    "time_context": "Studio lighting environment, timeless artistic setting"
  },
  "cinematography_and_tech": {
    "lighting": "Dual lighting setup: 1. Simulated shading within the sketch based on the reference. 2. External 'real world' harsh lamp light casting long shadows from the pencil and eraser onto the paper",
    "camera_gear": "Macro photography, 100mm lens, sharp focus on the paper texture",
    "framing": "Top-down flat lay or slight isometric angle to enhance the 'pop-up' 3D illusion of the sketch",
    "visual_fidelity": "Photorealistic rendering of paper grain/fiber, tactile graphite sheen, rough charcoal texture, high contrast between dark leads and white paper",
    "color_grading": "Monochromatic greyscale for the subject (graphite/charcoal tones), natural realistic colors for the desk and drawing tools"
  },
  "aspect_ratio": "4:5"
}
```

</div>

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```

  "model": "image_editing_pro",
  "task": "cinematic_aesthetic_portrait",
  "creative_direction": "Create a dreamy, romantic, and visually captivating portrait that feels calm, free, and effortlessly attractive, while preserving the original facial identity perfectly.",
  "reference_control": {
    "source": "attached_image",
    "face_identity": "strictly_preserved",
    "expression": "soft smile with peaceful, carefree emotion"
  },

    "appearance": "young woman with natural beauty, smooth skin, and delicate facial features",

    "styling_vibe": "minimal, natural, graceful charm"
  },
  "outfit_design": {
    "top": "off-shoulder soft knit sweater in {argument name="sweater color" default="light neutral tones"}, giving cozy yet feminine appeal",
    "overall_style": "casual elegance with subtle sensuality through posture and fabric flow"
  },
  "accessories": {
    "eyewear": "sleek stylish sunglasses reflecting warm sunset tones",
    "bag": "small shoulder bag adding lifestyle realism"
  },
  "pose_and_emotion": {
    "pose": "relaxed leaning posture, one hand resting naturally on railing",
    "mood": "free-spirited, joyful, emotionally warm"
  },
  "environment": {
    "location": "open waterfront during golden sunset",
    "elements": "flying seagulls, calm water surface, distant horizon creating depth",
    "atmosphere": "peaceful, airy, cinematic freedom"
  },
  "lighting_setup": {
    "light_type": "natural golden-hour sunlight",
    "effects": "warm highlights on skin, soft shadows, glowing sky reflections",
    "color_feel": "golden orange, pastel blue, soft sky gradients"
  },
  "camera_specs": {
    "lens": "35mm cinematic portrait",
    "angle": "slightly upward selfie perspective",
    "depth_of_field": "balanced focus with detailed foreground and airy background"
  },
  "quality_output": {
    "resolution": "8K",
    "detail_level": "high realism in skin, hair, water, and birds",
    "render_style": "premium cinematic photography"
  },
  "constraints": {
    "face_changes": "not_allowed",
    "beauty_filters": "disabled",
    "identity_shift": "zero_tolerance"
  },
  "final_goal": "A visually soothing, romantic, and aesthetically powerful image that feels alive, free, and naturally attractive without artificial exaggeration.",
```

### No. 79: Victorian Gothic Royal Portrait Magazine Cover Prompt

![Language-ZH](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-ZH-blue)

#### ğŸ“– Description

An extremely detailed, multi-section prompt for Nano Banana Pro to generate a 9:16 vertical, realistic magazine cover photo in a 'Victorian Gothic Royal' style. It requires 100% identity preservation from an uploaded face reference, specific heavy-duty Victorian court attire, London landmarks as the background, cinematic lighting, complex color matrix selection, and specific poses suitable for a magazine cover.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
Generate a 9:16 vertical, realistic photo of a "Victorian Gothic Royal" portrait: Use the uploaded FACE_REF as the character identity reference, 100% restoring the facial features and bone structure; the person is wearing heavy-duty court attire in the style of the "Victorian Era (19th Century) Court Gown" (corset, large crinoline, lace/velvet, royal jewelry), photographed next to the Tower Bridge or the Palace of Westminster (Big Ben) in London. The image should have photography, styling, and cover design quality comparable to 'Harperâ€™s Bazaar', maintaining the magazine's consistent design style (Chinese and English design).

ã€INPUTS | Inputã€‘
FACE_REF: Uploaded facial feature reference image (identity lock)

ã€ABSOLUTE PRIORITY | Identity Lock (Highest Priority)ã€‘
100% restoration of FACE_REF's facial features and bone structure: Eye distance, nose bridge and wings, lip shape, jawline, and cheekbone structure must be completely consistent, with no deviation.
Realistic skin texture: Visible subtle textures and pores; avoid excessive smoothing or 'influencer' filters.
Adult female image (adult).

ã€SHOT TYPE | Two View Options (Model randomly selects one, must be realistic and consistent)ã€‘
A) Half-body cover: From the chest to above the waist, with jewelry, lace neckline, and eyes being the clearest (Primary recommendation)
B) Full-body cover: Complete presentation from head to toe, showing the full silhouette of the huge crinoline combined with the London landmark, strong perspective (Alternative)
(Regardless of A/B: Must maintain a "cover composition," with white space reserved for typography, but without torn paper/hand-drawn effects.)

ã€LOCATION | Scene (London, UK)ã€‘
London Landmark: By the River Thames, with the magnificent Gothic architecture of the Palace of Westminster (Big Ben) or the Tower of London Bridge in the background.
Weather option (random): 1) London Fog (classic foggy texture, soft and mysterious light) 2) Just after rain (wet ground reflection, lead-gray sky)
Clean background: No tourists, no modern signs, no mobile phone status bar UI, no watermarks or subtitles.

ã€LIGHTING & CAMERA | Photographic Quality (Magazine Grade)ã€‘
Lens feel: 85mm portrait quality (half-body) or 50mm/70mm (full-body), shallow depth of field, eyes are the sharpest.
Lighting: Overcast diffused light + dramatic fill light (emphasizing facial structure); diamonds/gems must have realistic fire; velvet texture must be deep.
Color: High-end cinematic feel, low-saturation blue-gray environment combined with the dark tones of the clothing (red/blue/black) to form a Gothic aesthetic; overall clean, transparent, and luxurious.

ã€WARDROBE | Victorian Court Gown (Heavy-duty, Sculpting, Intricate Details)ã€‘
Target aesthetic: "Wasp waist, large skirt, layered lace, heavy velvet, crown, queenly aura."

Silhouette and Layers (X-shaped tailoring)
Upper body: Highly structured corset, square or high neckline, puff sleeves or leg-of-mutton sleeves
Lower body: Huge crinoline or bustle, with noticeable stacking design at the back waist, skirt trailing on the ground
Decoration: Abundant ruffles, bows, dangling tassels
Fabric and Craftsmanship (Heavy craftsmanship must be "visible")
Main fabric: Heavy velvet, taffeta, Chantilly Lace
Main techniques: Beading, gold thread embroidery, ribbon weaving
Pattern themes: Damask, roses, thistle (symbol of Scotland), paisley pattern
Details: Lace gloves, neck ornament (Choker), medal/brooch
Headwear (Royal Jewelry Headpiece)
Core structure: Victorian small crown (Tiara) or feather headpiece
Decoration: Diamonds, sapphires, pearls
Earrings/Necklace: Extremely exaggerated diamond necklace, drop earrings

ã€COLOR MATRIX | Color Matrix Pairing (Must be executed, and must be "Royal Dark Colors")ã€‘
(Deep luxury of the late Victorian era)
Randomly select 1 set from the following three "Main Color Schemes" for the [Base Color/Large Area Main Fabric Color].

Scheme G (Royal Blue Base):
Base Color: Deep sapphire blue/midnight blue (velvet texture)
Embroidery/Decoration: Silver lace, diamonds, sapphires
Scheme A (Victorian Red Base):
Base Color: Wine red/Burgundy red (deep passion)
Embroidery/Decoration: Black lace, gold embroidery, rubies
Scheme R (Mourning Black Base):
Base Color: Ink black (Black Jet, extremely Gothic)
Embroidery/Decoration: Black beads, black lace, small amounts of gold or silver highlights

ã€Color Execution Rulesã€‘
Colors must be deep and rich, reflecting the majesty of the "Empire on which the sun never sets" and Gothic mystery.

ã€POSE | Cover Pose (Majestic, Stiff, Queenly Aura)ã€‘
Half-body: Chin slightly raised, cold gaze, one hand gently touching the necklace
Full-body: Standing tall (like a portrait painting), hands clasped on the crinoline, overwhelming presence
Expression: Serious, arrogant, imperious; absolutely no smiling (Victorian style).

ã€OUTPUT | Outputã€‘
1 vertical 9:16 realistic magazine cover photo
Random: Half-body or Full-body (A/B selection)
Random: Fog or Rain (Weather selection)
Random: Sapphire Blue / Wine Red / Ink Black (Color matrix selection)
Styling: Victorian court gown direction + Crown/Choker + Corset and large crinoline + Velvet and lace
```

### No. 92: Polished Indoor Portrait with Shallow Depth of Field

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A detailed prompt for generating a photorealistic, polished portrait of a young Asian woman with glasses, seated in a leather armchair. The prompt specifies her outfit (pinstripe shirt dress, thigh-high stockings), pose (winking, hand near cheek), and precise camera settings (35mm/50mm, f/2.0-f/2.8) to achieve a shallow depth of field and warm indoor lighting.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
Subject: A photorealistic portrait of a young Asian woman with voluminous, long, wavy black hair and fair skin. She is wearing thin-rimmed, round glasses and has a playful expression, winking one eye with a subtle smile.
Outfit: She is dressed in a black, long-sleeved button-down shirt dress with thin white vertical pinstripes. She is wearing sheer black thigh-high stockings.
Pose: She is seated in a curved, cream-colored leather armchair. Her body is angled slightly forward. Her right hand is raised, with long manicured fingers delicately touching her cheek and jawline in a playful, posing gesture.
Environment: The background features soft, floor-length beige or off-white sheer curtains, suggesting an indoor hotel room or bedroom setting at night.
Lighting & Style: Warm, soft indoor lighting that creates gentle highlights on her hair and the silky texture of the shirt. High-resolution photography, sharp focus on the face, slightly candid but polished aesthetic.
Camera Angle: Slightly high angle (tilted down about 10â€“15 degrees), seated eye-level.
Focal Length: 35mm or 50mm. (This creates a natural perspective without too much distortion, typical of high-end smartphone portraits or standard portrait lenses).
Aperture: f/2.0 to f/2.8. (This provides a shallow depth of field, keeping her face and hand in sharp focus while softly blurring the texture of the curtains in the background).
Shutter Speed: 1/60s or 1/100s. (Standard for indoor handheld shots to avoid motion blur).
ISO: 400 to 800. (Slightly higher sensitivity to account for the warm, dim indoor lighting without introducing too much grain).
Lighting Setup: Soft key light from the front-top (likely a ceiling fixture or ring light), creating the specular highlights on the nose and forehead.
```

```
Body types: Extremely thin, slim, athletic, muscular, stocky, chubby, fat, plus-size, obese, petite, tall, short, broad-shouldered, narrow-framed, pear-shaped, apple-shaped, hourglass, rectangular, long-limbed, short-limbed.

Full spectrum of skin tones from the palest to the deepest.

Features: Freckles, vitiligo, acne, scars, birthmarks, moles, gap teeth, crooked teeth, big nose, small nose, wide nose, narrow nose, round face, angular face, soft jawline, strong jawline, monolid eyes, deep-set eyes, hooded eyes, big lips, thin lips, visible disabilities, prosthetics, wheelchair users, amputees.
Each cell: different pose, different camera angle. Poses should feel editorial and unexpectedâ€”leaning, crouching, mid-stride, arched, sprawled, seated, jumping, twisting, lounging. Camera angles varyâ€”low angle, overhead, Dutch tilt, wide shot, tight crop, ground-level, profile, three-quarter view.
Moody, high contrast, cinematic lighting. Varied environmentsâ€”studio, architectural, urban, natural. Sharp detail, clothing as focal point. Final result should feel like the most inclusive, human-rich fashion editorial ever createdâ€”a true celebration of every single type of human body that exists.
```

### No. 111: Image to Fragmented Stone Sculpture Style Transfer

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A structured JSON prompt for Nano Banana PRO to perform an image-to-image style transfer, transforming the main subject of an uploaded photo into a hyper-realistic, fragmented stone assemblage. It specifies material details (slate and sandstone shards), lighting (soft studio key light), and strict identity preservation.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
{
  "task": "image_to_image_style_transfer",
  "input_image": "{{USER_IMAGE}}",
  "prompt": "Create a hyper-real 3D studio composition that recreates the main subject from the provided image as a fragmented stone assemblage. The subject must be built from separate, clearly detached rock pieces with small visible gaps between shards (no pieces merging). Material look: fragmented slate + sandstone shards with chiseled edges, crisp fractures, visible stone grain, micro-scratches, and realistic roughness. Color palette: predominantly dark slate with subtle warm-ochre sandstone accents. Lighting: soft studio key light from top-left, gentle fill, subtle contact shadows under each shard, realistic ambient occlusion in crevices, clean reflections kept minimal. Background: minimal off-white seamless backdrop, no texture. Framing: centered, clean, straight-on, subject fully readable. Add a few tiny debris chips floating or resting near the base for depth. Preserve the subjectâ€™s identity, proportions, and recognizable silhouette from the input image while transforming all surfaces into stone fragments. Hyper-real, high detail, sharp focus, 8k render quality.",
  "negative_prompt": "text, typography, logo, watermark, signature, extra props, busy background, fog, heavy bloom, cartoon, illustration, lowpoly, plastic, metal, glossy paint, melted shapes, merged fragments, unreadable subject, blur, noise, low resolution, oversharpening halos, distorted face/body, extra limbs, deformed geometry",
  "output": {
    "aspect_ratio": "use_input_aspect_ratio",
    "background": "off_white",
    "camera": {
      "angle": "straight_on",
      "framing": "centered",
      "distance": "medium"
    }
  },
  "params": {
    "style_strength": 0.75,
    "identity_preservation": 0.9,
    "detail_level": "very_high",
    "lighting_preset": "soft_studio_top_left",
    "shadow_intensity": "subtle",
    "gap_visibility": "clear",
    "debris_chips": "few_tiny",
    "no_text": true
  }
}
```

##### Image 1

</div>

The surrounding organic elements visible in the image should influence how the miniature world integrates with the object, creating a believable coexistence between natural textures and engineered surfaces.

```
Ensure the figuresâ€™ interactions feel grounded and observational, subtly emphasizing structure, material weight, and mechanical precision without dramatization, glorification, or promotion. The scene should feel physically plausible, quiet, and lived-in.

Render with photorealistic depth, cinematic macro photography, shallow depth of field, micro-details, soft volumetric lighting, and seamless integration between characters and the object. The final composition should feel like a believable, tiny ecosystem existing on and within the object itself.
```

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A complex, multi-step system prompt that instructs the AI to act as a 'Streetwear Algorithm' to convert any random input object into a corresponding 'Hypebeast' fashion item (Puffer Jacket, Sneaker, Backpack, or Sunglasses) based on the object's physical properties (Texture, Structure, Shape). The prompt then requires generating a studio product shot of the resulting wearable, ensuring it looks manufactured from the input object's parts/materials.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
 Look at the attached image. Determine:
 Texture: ({argument name="texture options" default="Soft/Hard/Liquid/Glass"})
 Structure:  ({argument name="structure options" default="Rigid/Flexible/Mechanical"})
 Shape:  ({argument name="shape options" default="Boxy/Round/Aerodynamic/Flat"})
 2. AUTO-SELECT MODEL (Run this Logic Tree): 
 IF Input is Soft, Volumetric, or Tangled  (Noodles, Clouds, Moss, Bubblewrap)
 -> GENERATE: Oversized Puffer Jacket 
IF Input is Rigid, Aerodynamic, or Mechanical  (Stapler, Car, Power Tool, Robot)
 -> GENERATE: Chunky Conceptual Sneaker 
 IF Input is Boxy, Container-like, or Heavy Metal  (Safe, Trash Can, Speaker, Computer Case)
 -> GENERATE: Hard-Shell Tech Backpack 
 IF Input is Transparent, Glassy, or Thin/Wire-like  (Neon Sign, Circuit Board, Stained Glass, Ice)
 -> GENERATE: Futuristic Wrap-Around Sunglasses (Visor) 
 IF Input is Textile, Flat, or Pattern-Heavy** ({argument name="pattern input examples" default="Persian Rug, Painting, Cardboard"})
 -> GENERATE: Oversized Hoodie or Tactical Vest 
 
3. EXECUTE DESIGN: 
 Create a studio product shot of the "selected item".
 Design Rule:  The item must look like it was manufactured "using the parts/materials of the input object".
 Details:  Keep original branding/logos if present.
 Setting:  Floating pedestal, Cinematic Lighting, 8k Resolution.
```

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
Photorealistic ultra-wide desert scene in Egypt near the Giza plateau at golden hour. A colossal inverted pyramid, point-down, dominates the landscape at an unimaginable scale, dwarfing the horizon. Its vast upper rim stretches for multiple kilometers, while the sloping faces plunge inward toward a needle-like apex that hovers just above the sand, leaving a gigantic shadowed void beneath. The surface reads as ancient limestone blocks with dark granite inlays: mega-sized courses, eroded edges, wind-sanded wear, and long, faint bands of hieroglyphs that only appear where the sun grazes the stone. Include tiny scale cues in the distance: a thin line of tourists like ants, a few small buses and 4x4s parked far away, a camel caravan crossing the flats, and scattered survey flags. Heat haze and dust plumes soften the far edges. Sand dunes climb the lower planes where stone meets desert, with drifting sand spilling down seams like a slow waterfall. Pale sky, low sun, strong raking light, extreme HDR realism, crisp micro-textures, natural color grading, no glow or energy effects.
```

### No. 141: Logo to Floating Island Architectural Concept (4 Eras)

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A complex, multi-phase prompt instructing the AI to act as an Art Director and Brand Strategist. It takes an uploaded logo and transforms it into an architectural element of a futuristic logistics hub on a floating island, generating four distinct versions representing different historical/futuristic eras (Industrial Dawn, Golden Age, Hyper-Present, Solarpunk Future), while enforcing background color consistency.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
<instructions>Expert Art Director & Brand Strategist.
User uploads a logo (Transparent or Solid).

Phase 1: The Contrast Analysis
Step 1: Analyze the uploaded logo's brightness and dominant color.
Step 2: Select the ackground Strategy based on the rules below:
IF Logo is Dark/Black/Navy -> Set all backgrounds to "Solid Matte White (Hex #F5F5F7)".
IF Logo is Light/White/Silver/Yellow -> Set all backgrounds to "Deep Matte Charcoal (Hex #1A1A1A)".
IF Logo is Mid-tone/Colorful -> Set all backgrounds to "Soft Off-White (Hex #F0F0F0)" for maximum readability.

You must enforce the SAME background color prompt for all 4 eras to ensure Pitch Deck consistency.

Phase 2: The Visual Constants
Subject: A futuristic logistics hub on a floating island.
Style: Low-poly 3D render, Claymorphism (Clay UI).
Lighting:  Soft occlusion shadows, "Blender 3D" Cycle render, minimal texture.
Integration: The logo should not just be a billboard. It should be architectural (e.g., the shape of the building, the layout of the roads, or a giant hologram).

Phase 3: The 4 Eras (With Enforced Backgrounds)

Generate 4 Prompts using the Era themes below, but append the "Background Strategy" from Phase 1 to every single prompt. Draw them

1.  The Industrial Dawn (1890s): Brick, steam, brass, cobblestone.
2.  The Golden Age (1960s): Retro-futurism, curves, pastel accents (but keep background uniform).
3.  The Hyper-Present (2024): Glass, robotics, server racks, LEDs.
4.  The Solarpunk Future (2150): Organic white curves, trees, anti-gravity, wind power.
```

![Language-JA](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-JA-blue)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A detailed image generation prompt for Nano Banana Pro (using the Lovart model) to create a single, continuous panoramic digital illustration. The prompt emphasizes high detail, cinematic lighting, and 8K resolution.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
Ultra-realistic digital illustration: A view of the futuristic Skytree across the Sumida River from the historic Asakusa waterfront. Depict this scene seamlessly as a continuous composition showing the cycle of the four seasons.
The composition progresses naturally from left to right, flowing through Winter, Spring, Summer, and Autumn.
Left side (Winter): Cold snowy landscape, snow-covered historic buildings (Bund buildings), elements of ice and cloudy sky.
Center-left (Spring): Snow melting, fresh green sprouts, bright flowers like cherry blossoms and rapeseed flowers (image of Sumida River in Spring) in full bloom.
Center-right (Summer): Lush green vegetation, bright sunlight, strong reflections on the river surface, blue sky, and a vibrant summer scene.
Right side (Autumn): Vivid autumn colors of gold, orange, and red foliage, a late autumn scene with a harvest mood.
There are no visible boundaries between the seasons; the weather, lighting, and vegetation smoothly merge to form a unified and harmonious panorama. Express the rich details symbolizing the flow of time, cinematic lighting, 8K resolution, and extremely detailed textures.
```

### No. 153: 20-Panel Cartoon Robot Drawing Guide Prompt

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A detailed, step-by-step prompt for Nano Banana Pro (on LeonardoAi) instructing the model to create a 20-panel layout guide for drawing a cute cartoon robot, with each panel adding one specific, cumulative change, starting from basic guidelines to final details like claw hands and shadows.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
Create a 20-panel layout guide for drawing a cute cartoon robot. Each panel keeps everything from before and adds one clear change.

1. Light guide lines: vertical center, horizontal center, and a ground line.
2. Add torso: rounded rectangle above the ground.
3. Add torso centerline.
4. Add head: smaller rounded square above torso.
5. Add neck connector: short rounded block.
6. Add left eye circle.
7. Add right eye circle.
8. Add pupils inside both eyes.
9. Add thin rim rings around both eyes.
10. Add mouth rectangle below eyes.
11. Add evenly spaced vertical slats in the mouth.
12. Add left shoulder joint circle on torso side.
13. Add right shoulder joint circle.
14. Add left upper arm cylinder from left shoulder.
15. Add left elbow circle and left forearm cylinder.
16. Add left claw hand (base curve + two prongs).
17. Add right upper arm cylinder from right shoulder.
18. Add right elbow circle and right forearm cylinder.
19. Add right claw hand to match left.
20. Add legs and feet as simple blocks: two short legs from torso bottom and two rounded trapezoid feet, plus a small ground shadow.
```

#### ğŸ“– Description

A highly detailed prompt for Nano Banana Pro to convert characters in a reference image into watercolor illustrations of snowmen. It includes strict rules for the snowman's structure, the exclusion of human features, and the material rendering of the hair as pure white, compacted snow.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
# Describe the number, name, and appearance characteristics of the characters in the reference image here
[{argument name="Character Appearance" default="A girl wearing a cloak and a girl in a sailor uniform"}]

A watercolor illustration where all the above characters have transformed into cute â€œsnowmen.â€

- The bodies of all characters will take the shape of a â€œsnowman without limbs,â€ consisting of stacked white snowballs.
- The whole body is composed of 2 or 3 snowballs. Taller characters should have 3 segments.
- Eliminate human skin, limbs, and clothing details, making the body out of snow.
- To identify each character, only their characteristic â€œhats,â€ â€œribbons,â€ and â€œimage-colored buttons or scarvesâ€ should be attached to the snowman.
- The face should use simple snowman parts (black round eyes, orange or round nose).

â˜… Important Material Rule (Hair Correction):
- [Highest Priority] Hair parts must never be drawn as â€œhuman hairâ€ or â€œwigs.â€
- The shape of the hair is maintained, but the material is entirely â€œpure white snow mass.â€
- Completely ignore the original character's hair color (such as black or brown) and express it in the snow's original â€œsolid white (#FFFFFF).â€
- Do not draw individual strands of hair; depict it as a â€œsingle massâ€ of compacted snow.
- Eliminate the boundary between the head snowball and the hairstyle part, integrating them like a single large snow sculpture.
- The texture should not be smooth but should have the â€œroughnessâ€ and â€œunevennessâ€ characteristic of snow.
- The hair shape should be drawn as a â€œwhite silhouetteâ€ integrated with the snowman's head. The ends of the hair should not be sharp but rounded and plump, like melting snow.

Art Style:
- Analog-feeling watercolor painting.
- White drawing paper texture.
- Outlines are soft, and colors are pale and blurred.
- The background is white or a faint snowy landscape.
```

### No. 177: Exploded View Disassembly of Apple Watch Ultra and iPhone

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)

#### ğŸ“– Description

Two highly specific, technical prompts designed to generate exploded-view diagrams of Apple products (Watch Ultra and iPhone) based on a reference image. The prompts focus on maintaining perspective, lighting, and spatial realism while separating components in a controlled, orderly sequence.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
Apple Watch
Create a dynamic scene where the Apple Watch Ultra from Reference 1 breaks down into its individual components, with each piece leaving the dial in a controlled, forward-floating sequence that retains the original direction and perspective of the watch, maintaining the metallic finish, glass reflections, and rugged structure visible in the reference; place the detached orange strap behind the wrist while keeping the same soft, neutral studio lighting, the close-up composition of the arm, and the smooth muted background tone. Enhance micro-details, improve overall image fidelity, increase clarity, and make the colors more vibrant and saturated.

IPhone
Create a precise exploded-view animation of the Apple iPhone from Reference 1 where every internal and external layer, casing, glass, display, internal chips, modules, and structural parts, moves outward from the screen in a smooth, orderly chain, while keeping the same fixed viewpoint: a low frontal angle with the device vertical, right side slightly visible, left side largely hidden, the hand gripping the phone in the same position, and the soft diffused lighting unchanged; ensure each floating element is lit exactly like the main scene and casts subtle, accurate shadows onto adjacent parts and onto the hand, creating strong spatial realism without altering the composition. Enhance micro-details, improve overall image fidelity, increase clarity, and make the colors more vibrant and saturated.
```

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A highly specific JSON prompt for editing an existing image (face preservation enabled) into a tight close-up portrait illuminated by soft cinematic candlelight, detailing precise makeup specifications and demanding natural skin texture and minimal retouching.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
{
  "mode": "image_edit",
  "face_preservation": {
    "enabled": true,
    "strength": 1.0,
    "notes": "Face identity, proportions and features must remain completely unchanged"
  },
  "composition": {
    "shot_type": "tight close-up portrait",
    "camera_angle": "eye level",
    "framing": "centered face, symmetrical crop from forehead to lips",
    "expression": "soft, intimate expression, lips slightly parted, eyes looking sideways"
  },
  "lighting": {
    "type": "soft cinematic candle light",
    "key_light": "single candle flame from lower front side",
    "fill_light": "very subtle ambient bounce light",
    "contrast": "low",
    "highlights": "gentle glow on cheekbones and lips",
    "skin_detail": "natural texture preserved, visible pores"
  },
  "makeup": {
    "skin": {
      "base": "light natural foundation",
      "finish": "soft satin, skin-like",
      "freckles": "visible, not covered",
      "contour": "very soft natural contouring"
    },
    "eyes": {
      "eyeshadow": "warm nude and soft brown tones",
      "blending": "smooth and diffused",
      "eyeliner": "thin brown liner close to lash line",
      "lashes": "defined, natural volume, not dramatic",
      "brows": "natural brushed brows, softly defined"
    },
    "cheeks": {
      "blush": "soft peach / rose blush",
      "placement": "natural flush on cheeks"
    },
    "lips": {
      "color": "warm nude rose",
      "finish": "slightly glossy, hydrated",
      "definition": "natural lip shape, no overlining"
    }
  },
  "scene": {
    "props": ["single candle flame in foreground"],
    "background": "clean white minimal background",
    "depth_of_field": "shallow, candle softly blurred"
  },
  "style": {
    "mood": "intimate, cinematic, editorial beauty",
    "color_palette": "warm ivory, beige, soft peach",
    "retouching": "high-end editorial beauty retouch, no face reshaping"
  },
  "camera": {
    "lens": "85mm portrait lens",
    "aperture": "f1.8",
    "focus": "extremely sharp on eyes"
  },
  "negative_prompt": [
    "face change",
    "different identity",
    "plastic skin",
    "heavy makeup",
    "over-smoothing",
    "beauty filter",
    "AI artifacts"
  ]
}
```

A detailed prompt for Nano Banana Pro to create a cinematic, high-contrast close-up portrait of a woman with curly hair, featuring sharp shadows cast by palm fronds under the afternoon sun against a terracotta wall.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
Create a stunning close-up portrait of a woman with wild, curly hair, wearing a simple white tank top. She is leaning against a wall under the afternoon sun. The light is filtering through the leaves of a palm tree, casting sharp, high-contrast shadows of the fronds across her face and chest. One eye is illuminated by a patch of golden light, while the other is hidden in the leaf shadow. The background is a deep, shadowed terracotta wall. Cinematic, vibrant colors, sharp focus, sun-drenched aesthetic. Use aspect ratio 3:4.
```

### No. 196: K-Pop Idol Mirror Selfie in Dressing Room

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A highly technical prompt for generating an ultra-realistic mirror selfie of a K-pop idol aesthetic female subject. It specifies the exact pose (holding a smartphone), detailed outfit (cherry-red hair, white corset top), camera technical values (26mm, f/1.8, ISO 200), and the cool, high-key lighting of a backstage dressing room.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
"Young Asian female (K-pop idol aesthetic), pale porcelain skin, long straight dark cherry-red (burgundy) hair reaching waist length.",
      "apparel": {
        "top": "White strapless corset-style crop top with a central vertical zipper detail.",
        "bottom": "Matching white high-waisted mini skirt with vertical silver seam lines.",
        "sleeves": "Detached white opera-length arm warmers/gloves covering palms.",
        "jewelry": "Layered diamond choker necklaces with a pendant, dangling silver earrings, multiple silver rings."
      },
      "appearance": {
        "makeup": "Soft coral lip tint, subtle eyeliner, straight eyebrows.",
        "reflection": "The subject's back and long red hair are clearly visible in the large mirror behind her."
      }
    },
    "exact_pose_anatomical": {
      "type": "Standing Mirror Selfie.",
      "body_orientation": "Torso angled 45 degrees towards the mirror plane, hips shifted to the subject's right (creating a slight curve at the waist).",
      "head": "Turned to face the mirror directly, slight tilt to her left.",
      "right_arm": "Elbow bent, forearm raised, hand holding a white smartphone (iPhone Pro) up to shoulder height to capture the reflection.",
      "left_arm": "Extended downwards naturally by the side, hand relaxed.",
      "gaze": "Looking at the phone screen in the mirror."
    },
    "camera_technical_values": {
      "viewpoint": "Mirror reflection view (shot from the phone's perspective within the mirror).",
      "lens_focal_length": "26mm equivalent (Standard smartphone wide lens).",
      "aperture": "f/1.8 (Bright, sharp focus on the subject, slight fall-off in the deep background).",
      "shutter_speed": "1/100s (Indoor artificial light setting).",
      "iso": "ISO 200 (Clean image with minimal grain).",
      "framing": "Medium shot (Thighs up), capturing the subject and her reflection in the mirror."
    },
    "lighting_and_environment": {
      "environment": "Brightly lit backstage dressing room / makeup room.",
      "background_elements": "Large wall mirror, white countertop with black makeup cases, hair styling tools, cables, and a blurry reflection of chairs and white walls.",
      "lighting_type": "Cool White Artificial Fluorescence / Vanity Mirror Lighting.",
      "quality": "Flat, even illumination (high key), minimizing facial shadows, creating a clean and polished look.",
      "reflections": "Light glare on the phone case and glossy hair."
```

### No. 197: Cinematic Contact Sheet Generation from Reference Image

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A complex, multi-step prompt designed to generate a cohesive 3x3 cinematic contact sheet based on an uploaded reference image. It instructs the model to internalize the scene and subject, then create a sequence of images captured from multiple distances and angles while maintaining absolute consistency in subject, location, lighting, and emotional tone.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
Study the uploaded image carefully and fully internalize the scene: the subjectâ€™s appearance, clothing, posture, emotional state, and the surrounding environment. Treat this moment as a single frozen point in time.
Create a cinematic image set that feels like a photographer methodically explored this exact moment from multiple distances and angles, without changing anything about the subject or location.
All images must clearly belong to the same scene, captured under the same lighting conditions, weather, and atmosphere. Nothing in the world changes â€” only the camera position and framing evolve.
The emotional tone should remain consistent throughout the set, subtly expressed through posture, gaze, and micro-expressions rather than exaggerated acting.
Begin by observing the subject within the environment from afar, letting the surroundings dominate the frame and establish scale and mood.
Gradually move closer, allowing the subjectâ€™s full presence to emerge, then narrowing attention toward body language and facial expression.
End with intimate perspectives that reveal small but meaningful details â€” texture, touch, or eye focus â€” before shifting perspective above and below the subject to suggest reflection, vulnerability, or quiet resolve.
Across the sequence:
Wider views should emphasize space and atmosphere
Mid-range views should emphasize posture and emotional context
Close views should isolate feeling and detail
Perspective shifts (low and high angles) should feel purposeful and cinematic, not decorative
Depth of field must behave naturally: distant views remain mostly sharp, while closer frames introduce shallow focus and gentle background separation.
The final result should read as a cohesive 3Ã—3 cinematic contact sheet, as if selected from a single roll of film documenting one emotional moment from multiple viewpoints.
No text, symbols, signage, watermarks, numbers, or graphic elements may appear anywhere in the images.
Photorealistic rendering, cinematic color grading, and consistent visual realism are mandatory.
```

### No. 198: Nighttime Poolside Vacation Photo Analysis Prompt

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A detailed JSON prompt structured for image analysis, describing a young woman lying on her stomach in a resort pool at night. The prompt specifies the subject's pose, expression, clothing, and the tropical environment, focusing on high-contrast flash photography lighting for a playful, vacation-themed image.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
{
  "image_analysis": {
    "subject": {
      "demographics": "Young woman",
      "pose": "Lying on stomach in pool, propped up on elbows, legs bent upward at the knees with feet crossed in the air",
      "expression": "Broad, cheerful smile, looking directly at the camera",
      "hair": "Dark, wet, slicked back from swimming",
      "clothing": {
        "item": "One-piece swimsuit",
        "color": "Purple"
      }
    },
    "environment": {
      "location": "Outdoor swimming pool at a resort or hotel",
      "time_of_day": "Night",
      "weather": "Clear, tropical",
      "background": {
        "elements": [
          "Tall palm trees",
          "Multi-story hotel building with warm lights in windows",
          "Dark night sky"
        ]
      },
      "foreground": {
        "elements": [
          "Rippled blue pool water",
          "Reflection of the subject in the water"
        ]
      }
    },
    "lighting": {
      "style": "Flash photography mixed with ambient background light",
      "qualities": [
        "Subject is brightly illuminated",
        "Background is dimly lit with warm accent lights",
        "High contrast between subject and dark background"
      ]
    },
    "aesthetics": {
      "mood": "Happy, playful, relaxed, vacation vibes",
      "composition": "Eye-level shot relative to the water surface, subject centered",
      "color_palette": [
        "Purple (swimsuit)",
        "Deep Cyan/Blue (water)",
        "Black (sky)",
        "Warm Yellow/Orange (background lights)",
        "Green (palm trees)"
      ]
    }
  }
}
```

### No. 200: 16K Cinematic Night Portrait with Strict Identity Lock

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A highly detailed JSON prompt for Nano Banana Pro, focused on generating a 16K ultra-high-resolution, hyper-realistic cinematic night portrait of a male subject. The prompt enforces a strict identity lock based on an uploaded image, placing the subject in a modern urban night setting with cool cyan and teal cinematic lighting, aiming for a quiet luxury aesthetic.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
{
  "type": "image_generation_prompt",
  "style": "16K ultra-high-resolution, hyper-realistic, cinematic, premium realism",

  "identity_preservation": {
    "use_uploaded_image": true,
    "alter_face": false,
    "notes": "Strict identity lock. Preserve exact facial structure, skin tone, beard shape, eye placement, and hairline. Face must remain fully recognizable and natural. No beautification."
  },

  "subject": {
    "gender": "male",
    "pose": "standing naturally, relaxed and confident",
    "expression": "subtle half-smile, calm, approachable"
  },

  "wardrobe": {
    "outerwear": "tailored dark jacket or overshirt in black, charcoal, or deep navy",
    "inner_layer": "minimal plain tee or knit",
    "fit": "clean, structured, premium",
    "branding": "no logos"
  },

  "environment": {
    "location": "modern urban night setting",
    "background": "softly blurred city lights and skyline, believable and present-day",
    "air": "clear night air, no fog or haze"
  },

  "lighting": {
    "setup": "cinematic night lighting with soft frontal key light and subtle rim light",
    "color_tone": "cool cyan and teal with very subtle magenta accents",
    "characteristics": "balanced exposure, deep controlled shadows, no glow"
  },

  "camera": {
    "lens": "85mm cinematic portrait lens",
    "framing": "chest-up portrait",
    "depth_of_field": "soft background separation",
    "focus": "tack-sharp on face"
  },
  
  "quality": {
    "realism": "ultra-realistic",
    "skin": "natural pores and micro-texture",
    "materials": "physically accurate fabric and lighting interaction"
  },

  "mood": "quiet luxury, relaxed confidence, cinematic",

  "output_goal": "A 16K ultra-realistic cinematic night portrait that feels like a high-end luxury brand campaign while perfectly preserving the subjectâ€™s exact identity."
}
```

## ğŸ¤ How to Contribute

We welcome contributions! You can submit prompts via:

### ğŸ› GitHub Issue

1. Click [**Submit New Prompt**](https://github.com/YouMind-OpenLab/awesome-nano-banana-pro-prompts/issues/new?template=submit-prompt.yml)
2. Fill in the form with prompt details and image
3. Submit and wait for team review
4. If approved (we'll add `approved` label), it will automatically sync to CMS
5. Your prompt will appear in README within 4 hours

**Note:** We only accept submissions via GitHub Issues to ensure quality control.

See [CONTRIBUTING.md](docs/CONTRIBUTING.md) for detailed guidelines.
